# `RoutingAPI` Class

Queues, wrapup codes, skills, email & sms config, predictive routing

## Methods

- [`deleteRoutingAssessment`](#deleteroutingassessment) - Delete single benefit assessment.
- [`deleteRoutingDirectroutingbackupSettingsMe`](#deleteroutingdirectroutingbackupsettingsme) - Delete the user's Direct Routing Backup settings and revert to the Direct Routing Queue default.
- [`deleteRoutingEmailDomain`](#deleteroutingemaildomain) - Delete a domain
- [`deleteRoutingEmailDomainRoute`](#deleteroutingemaildomainroute) - Delete a route
- [`deleteRoutingEmailOutboundDomain`](#deleteroutingemailoutbounddomain) - Delete an outbound domain
- [`deleteRoutingLanguage`](#deleteroutinglanguage) - Delete a routing language
- [`deleteRoutingPredictor`](#deleteroutingpredictor) - Delete single predictor.
- [`deleteRoutingQueue`](#deleteroutingqueue) - Delete a queue
- [`deleteRoutingQueueMember`](#deleteroutingqueuemember) - Delete a queue member.
- [`deleteRoutingQueueUser`](#deleteroutingqueueuser) - DEPRECATED: use DELETE /routing/queues/{queueId}/members/{memberId}.  Delete queue member.
- [`deleteRoutingQueueWrapupcode`](#deleteroutingqueuewrapupcode) - Delete a wrap-up code from a queue
- [`deleteRoutingSettings`](#deleteroutingsettings) - Delete an organization's routing settings
- [`deleteRoutingSkill`](#deleteroutingskill) - Delete Routing Skill
- [`deleteRoutingSkillgroup`](#deleteroutingskillgroup) - Remove skill group definition
- [`deleteRoutingSmsAddress`](#deleteroutingsmsaddress) - Delete an Address by Id for SMS
- [`deleteRoutingSmsPhonenumber`](#deleteroutingsmsphonenumber) - Delete a phone number provisioned for SMS.
- [`deleteRoutingUserDirectroutingbackupSettings`](#deleteroutinguserdirectroutingbackupsettings) - Delete the user's Direct Routing Backup settings and revert to the Direct Routing Queue default.
- [`deleteRoutingUserUtilization`](#deleteroutinguserutilization) - Delete the user's max utilization settings and revert to the organization-wide default.
- [`deleteRoutingUtilization`](#deleteroutingutilization) - Delete the organization-wide max utilization settings and revert to the system default.
- [`deleteRoutingUtilizationLabel`](#deleteroutingutilizationlabel) - Delete a utilization label
- [`deleteRoutingWrapupcode`](#deleteroutingwrapupcode) - Delete wrap-up code
- [`deleteUserRoutinglanguage`](#deleteuserroutinglanguage) - Remove a routing language from a user
- [`deleteUserRoutingskill`](#deleteuserroutingskill) - Remove a routing skill from a user
- [`getRoutingAssessment`](#getroutingassessment) - Retrieve a single benefit assessment.
- [`getRoutingAssessments`](#getroutingassessments) - Retrieve all benefit assessments.
- [`getRoutingAssessmentsJob`](#getroutingassessmentsjob) - Retrieve a single benefit assessmentsÂ job.
- [`getRoutingAssessmentsJobs`](#getroutingassessmentsjobs) - Retrieve all benefit assessment jobs.
- [`getRoutingAvailablemediatypes`](#getroutingavailablemediatypes) - Get available media types

- [`getRoutingEmailOutboundDomainActivation`](#getroutingemailoutbounddomainactivation) - Get activation status (cname + dkim) of an outbound domain
- [`getRoutingEmailOutboundDomains`](#getroutingemailoutbounddomains) - Get outbound domains

- [`getRoutingQueuesDivisionviewsAll`](#getroutingqueuesdivisionviewsall) - Get a paged listing of simplified queue objects, sorted by name.  Can be used to get a digest of all queues in an organization.
- [`getRoutingQueuesMe`](#getroutingqueuesme) - Get a paged listing of queues the user is a member of.

- [`putUserRoutingskillsBulk`](#putuserroutingskillsbulk) - Assign multiple routing skills to a user, replacing any current assignments

### `deleteRoutingAssessment`

Delete single benefit assessment.

#### Endpoint

`DELETE /api/v2/routing/assessments/{assessmentId}`

#### Parameters

- `assessmentId` - **(string, required)** Benefit Assessment ID

#### Returns

A promise that settles to an [`HTTPResponse`](https://github.com/jfabello/http-client) object with the response of the call to the API endpoint. The promise fulfills if the HTTP status code is between 200 and 299. The promise rejects for any other HTTP status code.

| HTTP Status Code | Returned type | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `204` |  | Deleted successfully |
| `400` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request could not be understood by the server due to malformed syntax. |
| `401` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | No authentication bearer token specified in authorization header. |
| `403` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | You are not authorized to perform the requested action. |
| `404` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The requested resource was not found. |
| `408` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The client did not produce a request within the server timeout limit. This can be caused by a slow network connection and/or large payloads. |
| `409` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request conflicts with the current state of the target resource. |
| `413` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request is over the size limit. Maximum bytes: %s |
| `415` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Unsupported Media Type - Unsupported or incorrect media type, such as an incorrect Content-Type value in the header. |
| `429` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Rate limit exceeded the maximum. Retry the request in [%s] seconds |
| `500` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The server encountered an unexpected condition which prevented it from fulfilling the request. |
| `503` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Service Unavailable - The server is currently unavailable (because it is overloaded or down for maintenance). |
| `504` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request timed out. |

### `deleteRoutingDirectroutingbackupSettingsMe`

#### Endpoint

`DELETE /api/v2/routing/directroutingbackup/settings/me`

#### Parameters

This method does not have any parameters.

#### Returns

### `deleteRoutingEmailDomainRoute`

`DELETE /api/v2/routing/email/domains/{domainName}/routes/{routeId}`

#### Parameters

- `domainName` - **(string, required)** email domain
- `routeId` - **(string, required)** route ID

#### Returns

A promise that settles to an [`HTTPResponse`](https://github.com/jfabello/http-client) object with the response of the call to the API endpoint. The promise fulfills if the HTTP status code is between 200 and 299. The promise rejects for any other HTTP status code.

| HTTP Status Code | Returned type | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `200` |  | Route deletion completed. |

| `409` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request conflicts with the current state of the target resource. |

### `deleteRoutingPredictor`

Delete single predictor.

#### Endpoint

`DELETE /api/v2/routing/predictors/{predictorId}`

#### Parameters

- `predictorId` - **(string, required)** Predictor ID

#### Returns

A promise that settles to an [`HTTPResponse`](https://github.com/jfabello/http-client) object with the response of the call to the API endpoint. The promise fulfills if the HTTP status code is between 200 and 299. The promise rejects for any other HTTP status code.

| HTTP Status Code | Returned type | Description |
|---|---|---|

#### Endpoint

`GET /api/v2/routing/queues`

#### Parameters

- `query` - **(object)** The query string parameters for the request. An empty object or `null` is allowed if all query string parameters are optional.
- `query.pageNumber` - **(number, optional)** Page number
- `query.pageSize` - **(number, optional)** Page size
- `query.sortOrder` - **(string, optional)** Note: results are sorted by name.
- `query.name` - **(string, optional)** Include only queues with the given name (leading and trailing asterisks allowed)
- `query.id` - **(string[], optional)** Include only queues with the specified ID(s)
- `query.divisionId` - **(string[], optional)** Include only queues in the specified division ID(s)
- `query.peerId` - **(string[], optional)** Include only queues with the specified peer ID(s)
- `query.cannedResponseLibraryId` - **(string, optional)** Include only queues explicitly associated with the specified canned response library ID
- `query.hasPeer` - **(boolean, optional)** Include only queues with a peer ID

#### Returns

A promise that settles to an [`HTTPResponse`](https://github.com/jfabello/http-client) object with the response of the call to the API endpoint. The promise fulfills if the HTTP status code is between 200 and 299. The promise rejects for any other HTTP status code.

| HTTP Status Code | Returned type | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `200` | [QueueEntityListing](../definitions/queueentitylisting-definition.md) | successful operation |
| `400` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request could not be understood by the server due to malformed syntax. |
| `401` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | No authentication bearer token specified in authorization header. |
| `403` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | You are not authorized to perform the requested action. |
| `404` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The requested resource was not found. |
| `408` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The client did not produce a request within the server timeout limit. This can be caused by a slow network connection and/or large payloads. |
| `409` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request conflicts with the current state of the target resource. |
| `413` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request is over the size limit. Maximum bytes: %s |
| `415` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Unsupported Media Type - Unsupported or incorrect media type, such as an incorrect Content-Type value in the header. |
| `429` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Rate limit exceeded the maximum. Retry the request in [%s] seconds |
| `500` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The server encountered an unexpected condition which prevented it from fulfilling the request. |
| `503` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Service Unavailable - The server is currently unavailable (because it is overloaded or down for maintenance). |
| `504` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request timed out. |

### `getRoutingSmsAvailablephonenumbers`

Get a list of available phone numbers for SMS provisioning.

#### Description

This request will return up to 30 random phone numbers matching the criteria specified.  To get additional phone numbers repeat the request.

#### Endpoint

`GET /api/v2/routing/sms/availablephonenumbers`

#### Parameters

- `query` - **(object)** The query string parameters for the request. An empty object or `null` is allowed if all query string parameters are optional.
- `query.countryCode` - **(string, required)** The ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 country code of the county for which available phone numbers should be returned
- `query.region` - **(string, optional)** Region/province/state that can be used to restrict the numbers returned
- `query.city` - **(string, optional)** City that can be used to restrict the numbers returned
- `query.areaCode` - **(string, optional)** Area code that can be used to restrict the numbers returned
- `query.phoneNumberType` - **(string, required)** Type of available phone numbers searched
- `query.pattern` - **(string, optional)** A pattern to match phone numbers. Valid characters are '*' and [0-9a-zA-Z]. The '*' character will match any single digit.
- `query.addressRequirement` - **(string, optional)** This indicates whether the phone number requires to have an Address registered.

#### Returns

A promise that settles to an [`HTTPResponse`](https://github.com/jfabello/http-client) object with the response of the call to the API endpoint. The promise fulfills if the HTTP status code is between 200 and 299. The promise rejects for any other HTTP status code.

| HTTP Status Code | Returned type | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `200` | [SMSAvailablePhoneNumberEntityListing](../definitions/smsavailablephonenumberentitylisting-definition.md) | successful operation |
| `400` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request could not be understood by the server due to malformed syntax. |
| `401` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | No authentication bearer token specified in authorization header. |
| `403` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | You are not authorized to perform the requested action. |
| `404` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The requested resource was not found. |
| `408` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The client did not produce a request within the server timeout limit. This can be caused by a slow network connection and/or large payloads. |
| `409` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request conflicts with the current state of the target resource. |
| `413` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request is over the size limit. Maximum bytes: %s |
| `415` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Unsupported Media Type - Unsupported or incorrect media type, such as an incorrect Content-Type value in the header. |
| `429` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Rate limit exceeded the maximum. Retry the request in [%s] seconds |

### `getRoutingSmsPhonenumbers`

Get a list of provisioned phone numbers.

#### Endpoint

`GET /api/v2/routing/sms/phonenumbers`

#### Parameters

- `query` - **(object)** The query string parameters for the request. An empty object or `null` is allowed if all query string parameters are optional.
- `query.phoneNumber` - **(string, optional)** Filter on phone number address. Allowable characters are the digits '0-9' and the wild card character '\*'. If just digits are present, a contains search is done on the address pattern. For example, '317' could be matched anywhere in the address. An '\*' will match multiple digits. For example, to match a specific area code within the US a pattern like '1317*' could be used.
- `query.phoneNumberType` - **(string[], optional)** Filter on phone number type
- `query.phoneNumberStatus` - **(string[], optional)** Filter on phone number status
- `query.countryCode` - **(string[], optional)** Filter on country code
- `query.pageSize` - **(number, optional)** Page size
- `query.pageNumber` - **(number, optional)** Page number
- `query.sortBy` - **(string, optional)** Optional field to sort results
- `query.sortOrder` - **(string, optional)** Sort order
- `query.language` - **(string, optional)** A language tag (which is sometimes referred to as a "locale identifier") to use to localize country field and sort operations
- `query.integration.id` - **(string, optional)** Filter on the Genesys Cloud integration id to which the phone number belongs to
- `query.supportedContent.id` - **(string, optional)** Filter based on the supported content ID

#### Returns

A promise that settles to an [`HTTPResponse`](https://github.com/jfabello/http-client) object with the response of the call to the API endpoint. The promise fulfills if the HTTP status code is between 200 and 299. The promise rejects for any other HTTP status code.

| HTTP Status Code | Returned type | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `200` | [SmsPhoneNumberEntityListing](../definitions/smsphonenumberentitylisting-definition.md) | successful operation |
| `400` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request could not be understood by the server due to malformed syntax. |
| `401` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | No authentication bearer token specified in authorization header. |
| `403` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | You are not authorized to perform the requested action. |
| `404` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The requested resource was not found. |
| `408` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The client did not produce a request within the server timeout limit. This can be caused by a slow network connection and/or large payloads. |
| `409` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request conflicts with the current state of the target resource. |
| `413` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request is over the size limit. Maximum bytes: %s |
| `415` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Unsupported Media Type - Unsupported or incorrect media type, such as an incorrect Content-Type value in the header. |
| `429` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | Rate limit exceeded the maximum. Retry the request in [%s] seconds |

### `postRoutingEmailDomainTestconnection`

Tests the custom SMTP server integration connection set on this domain

#### Description

The request body is optional. If omitted, this endpoint will just test the connection of the Custom SMTP Server. If the body is specified, there will be an attempt to send an email message to the server.

#### Endpoint

`POST /api/v2/routing/email/domains/{domainId}/testconnection`

#### Parameters

- `domainId` - **(string, required)** domain ID
- `body` - **([TestMessage](../definitions/testmessage-definition.md), optional)** - The body of the request. An empty object or `null` is allowed if the body is optional.

#### Returns

A promise that settles to an [`HTTPResponse`](https://github.com/jfabello/http-client) object with the response of the call to the API endpoint. The promise fulfills if the HTTP status code is between 200 and 299. The promise rejects for any other HTTP status code.

| HTTP Status Code | Returned type | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `200` | [TestMessage](../definitions/testmessage-definition.md) | successful operation |
| `400` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request could not be understood by the server due to malformed syntax. |
| `401` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | No authentication bearer token specified in authorization header. |
| `403` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | You are not authorized to perform the requested action. |
| `404` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The requested resource was not found. |
| `408` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The client did not produce a request within the server timeout limit. This can be caused by a slow network connection and/or large payloads. |
| `409` | [ErrorBody](../definitions/errorbody-definition.md) | The request conflicts with the current state of the target resource. |
